   <script>
    function openMenu(menuid) {
    $('.'+menuid).toggle();
}
function showMobFilters() {
    $('#panel').append('<div class="filter-overlay"></div>');
    $('#mobmenufilters').show();
}
$('#mobmenufilters a').on('click',function() {
    $('.mobilefiltermenu').hide();
    $('#mobmenu'+$(this).attr('data-menu')).show();
});
   </script>

     <script>
      $('.th-sort-results').on('click',function() {
    var curloc = window.location.href;
    if(curloc.indexOf('order=') == -1) {
        if(curloc.indexOf('?') == -1) {
            newloc = curloc+'?page=0&order='+$(this).attr('data-field')+'&s='+$(this).attr('data-sort');
        }
        else {
            newloc = curloc+'&order='+$(this).attr('data-field')+'&s='+$(this).attr('data-sort');
        }
    }
    else {
        newloc = curloc.replace('order='+$('[name="order"]').val(),'order='+$(this).attr('data-field'));
        newloc = newloc.replace('s='+$('[name="s"]').val(),'s='+$(this).attr('data-sort'));
    }
    window.location = newloc;
});
function searchClubsNav(tx) {
    if(tx != '') {
        $('.teamdroprightheader').hide();
        $('.mobilefilter-subheader').hide();
        $('.mobilefiltermenu-submenu').hide();
        $('.hiddenteam').each(function() {
            $(this).hide();
            if($(this).data('clubname').toLowerCase().indexOf(tx.toLowerCase()) != -1) {
                $(this).attr('style','display:block !important;');
                $(this).html('<img src="/assets/img/fifa23/badges/'+$(this).attr('data-id')+'.png" style="width:20px;vertical-align: middle;margin-top: -2px;"> '+$(this).attr('data-clubname'));
            }
        });
    }
    else {
        $('.hiddenteam').attr('style','');
        $('.teamdroprightheader').show();
        $('.mobilefilter-subheader').show();
    }
}
function searchClubsMob(tx) {
    if(tx != '') {
        $('.teamdroprightheader').hide();
        $('.mobilefilter-subheader').hide();
        $('.mobilefiltermenu-submenu').hide();
        $('.hiddenteammob').each(function() {
            $(this).hide();
            if($(this).data('clubname').toLowerCase().indexOf(tx.toLowerCase()) != -1) {
                $(this).attr('style','display:block !important;');
                $(this).html('<img src="/assets/img/fifa23/badges/'+$(this).attr('data-id')+'.png" style="width:20px;vertical-align: middle;margin-top: -2px;"> '+$(this).attr('data-clubname'));
            }
        });
    }
    else {
        $('.hiddenteammob').attr('style','');
        $('.teamdroprightheader').show();
        $('.mobilefilter-subheader').show();
    }
}
function applyRating(ex='') {
    gotourl = '/en/fifa23/players?page=0';
    if($('.minratingnav'+ex).val() != '') {
        gotourl+= '&minrating='+$('.minratingnav'+ex).val();
    }
    if($('.maxratingnav'+ex).val() != '') {
        gotourl+= '&maxrating='+$('.maxratingnav'+ex).val();
    }
    window.location = gotourl;
}
function applyBin(ex='') {
    gotourl = '/en/fifa23/players?page=0';
    if($('.minbin'+ex).val() != '') {
        gotourl+= '&minprice='+$('.minbin'+ex).val();
    }
    if($('.maxbin'+ex).val() != '') {
        gotourl+= '&maxprice='+$('.maxbin'+ex).val();
    }
    window.location = gotourl;
}

    }
    if($('.maxagenav'+ex).val() != '') {

function applyStats(ex='') {
    gotourl = '/en/fifa23/players?page=0';
    if($('.accelerate').val() != 0) {
        gotourl+='&accelerate='+$('.accelerate').val();
    }
    if($('.minatt1'+ex).val() == 0 && $('.maxatt1'+ex).val() == 99) {
    }
    else {
            gotourl+='&minatt1='+$('.minatt1'+ex).val()+'&maxatt1='+$('.maxatt1'+ex).val();
        }
        if($('.minatt2'+ex).val() == 0 && $('.maxatt2'+ex).val() == 99) {

$('.togglecards').on('click',function() {
    if($(this).attr('data-toggle') == 'off') {
        $('#cardview').show();
        $('.playersearchresults').hide();
        $('.togglecards').html('Cards <i class="fa fa-toggle-on"></i>');
        $(this).attr('data-toggle','on');
    }
    else if($(this).attr('data-toggle') == 'on') {
        $('#cardview').hide();
        $('.playersearchresults').show();
        $('.togglecards').html('Cards <i class="fa fa-toggle-off"></i>');
        $(this).attr('data-toggle','off');
    }
});
$('.futversion').val('FUT 23');

function setDview() {
    if(localStorage.showdesktop == 'true'){
        $("meta[name=viewport]").attr('content', 'width=1440, initial-scale=1.0');
        setTimeout(function() { $('.switchtomoblink').show(); },1000);
    }
    if(typeof localStorage.showdesktop === 'undefined') {
        $('.switchtomoblink').hide();
    }
}
